 mri_label2label --srcsubject fsaverage --srclabel /gpfs/projects/dsnlab/shared/tag/bids_data/derivatives/freesurfer6/fsaverage/label/rh.BA1_exvivo.label --trgsubject sub-TAG147 --trglabel ./rh.BA1_exvivo.label --hemi rh --regmethod surface

trghemi = rh
trgsurface = white

trgsurfreg = sphere.reg
usehash = 1
Use ProjAbs  = 0, 0
Use ProjFrac = 0, 0
